Question #2 (ID: 311539)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math](x-11)[/math] এবং [math](x + 5)[/math] এর গুণফল নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]x^{2}-6 x+55[/math]
খ. [math]x^{2}+6 x-55[/math]
গ. [math]x^{2}+6 x+55[/math]
ঘ. [math]x^{2}-6 x-55[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]x^{2}-6 x-55[/math]

Solution:
[math](x-11)(x+5)=x^{2}+(-11+5) x+(-11)(5)=x^{2}-6 x-55[/math]

Question #3 (ID: 311540)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{6}[/math] হলে [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]4[/math]
C. [math]32[/math]
D. [math]40[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(x-\frac{\Gamma}{x}\right)^{2}=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=(\sqrt{6})^{2}-4=6-4=2[/math]

Explanation:

Question #4 (ID: 311541)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x-\frac{1}{x}=5[/math] হলে, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{21}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{23}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{27}[/math]
D. [math]\sqrt{29}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\sqrt{29}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}+4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=5^{2}+4=29 \therefore x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{29}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #5 (ID: 311542)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]m-\frac{1}{m}=4[/math] হলে, [math]\left(m+\frac{1}{m}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]20[/math]
B. [math]18[/math]
C. [math]14[/math]
D. [math]12[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]20[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(m+\frac{1}{m}\right)^{2}=\left(m-\frac{1}{m}\right)^{2}+4 \cdot m \cdot \frac{1}{m}=4^{2}+4=20[/math]

Question #6 (ID: 311543)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=10[/math] হলে, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{6}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]
গ. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{14}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=10+2=12[/math]
 [math]\therefore x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{12}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #7 (ID: 311544)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a=x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] এবং [math]b=\frac{1}{x}-x,[/math] হলে, [math](a - b)² =[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]2x[/math]
B. [math]4x[/math]
C. [math]4 x^{2}[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]4 x^{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]a-b=x+\frac{1}{x}-\frac{1}{x}+x=2 x \quad \therefore(a-b)^{2}=(2 x)^{2}=4 x^{2}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #8 (ID: 311545)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p + q = 7[/math] এবং [math]pq = 9[/math] হলে, [math]p² + q^{2}[/math] এর মান কোনটি? (মধ্যম)

Options:
ক. [math]67[/math]
খ. [math]40[/math]
গ. [math]31[/math]
ঘ. [math]13[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]31[/math]

Solution:
[math]p^{2}+q^{2}=(p+q)^{2}-2 p q=7^{2}-2 \times 9=49-18=31[/math]

Explanation:

Question #9 (ID: 311546)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x + y = 6[/math] এবং [math]xy= 4[/math] হলে [math]5xy[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]16[/math]
খ. [math]14[/math]
গ. [math]25[/math]
ঘ. [math]36[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]25[/math]

Solution:
[math]5 x y=\frac{5}{4} \times 4 x y=\frac{5}{4}[/math]
 [math]\left\{(x+y)^{2}-(x-y)^{2}\right\}=\frac{5}{4}\left(6^{2}-4^{2}\right)=\frac{5}{4} \times 20=25[/math]


Explanation:

Question #10 (ID: 311547)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x + y = 7[/math] এবং [math]xy = 12[/math] হলে, [math]2(x - y)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]1[/math]
খ. [math]2[/math]
গ. [math]25[/math]
ঘ. [math]75[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]2(x-y)^{2}=2\left\{(x+y)^{2}-4 x y\right\}=2\left(7^{2}-4 \times 12\right)=2(49-48)=2[/math]

Explanation:

Question #11 (ID: 311548)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x + y = 3[/math] এবং [math]x - y = - 1[/math] হলে [math]xy[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]-1[/math]
খ. [math]-2[/math]
গ. [math]2[/math]
ঘ. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]x y=\frac{(x+y)^{2}-(x-y)^{2}}{4}=\frac{3^{2}-(-1)^{2}}{4}=\frac{9-1}{4}=\frac{8}{4}=2[/math]

Explanation:

Question #12 (ID: 311549)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}-\sqrt{5} x+1=0[/math] হলে, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}= কত[/math]

Options:
A. [math]2 \sqrt{5}[/math]
B. [math]-\sqrt{5}[/math]
C. [math]\sqrt{5}[/math]
D. [math]5 \sqrt{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\sqrt{5}[/math]

Solution:
[math]x^{2}-\sqrt{5} x+1=0[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}+1=\sqrt{5} x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{x^{2}}{x}+\frac{1}{x}=\frac{\sqrt{5} x}{x} \therefore x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{5}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #13 (ID: 311550)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}-4 x-1=0[/math] হলে, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কত? যখন, [math]x 
eq 0[/math]

Options:
A. [math]-4[/math]
B. [math]-1[/math]
C. [math]4[/math]
D. [math]16[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]16[/math]

Solution:
[math]x^{2}-4 x-1=0 \Rightarrow x^{2}-1=4 x \Rightarrow \frac{x^{2}-1}{x}=4[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow x-\frac{1}{x}=4 \Rightarrow\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=4^{2}=16[/math]


Explanation:

Question #14 (ID: 311551)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^{2}-3 a-1=0[/math] হলে, [math]a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]5[/math]
খ. [math]7[/math]
গ. [math]11[/math]
ঘ. [math]13[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]11[/math]

Solution:
[math]a^{2}-3 a-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}-1=3 a[/math]
বা, [math]a-\frac{1}{a}=3[/math]
বা, [math]\left(a-\frac{i}{a}\right)^{2}=3^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}-2 a \cdot \frac{1}{a}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=9 \quad \therefore a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=11[/math]


Explanation:

Question #15 (ID: 311552)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]m^{2}-6 m-1=0[/math] হলে, [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=[/math] = কত

Options:
A. [math]32[/math]
B. [math]34[/math]
C. [math]36[/math]
D. [math]38[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]38[/math]

Solution:
[math]m^{2}-6 m-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}-1=6 m[/math]
বা, [math]m-\frac{1}{m}=6[/math]
বা, [math]\left(m-\frac{1}{m}\right)^{2}=6^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\mathrm{m}^{2}-2 \mathrm{~m} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}^{2}}=36^{\circ} \therefore \mathrm{m}^{2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}^{2}}=38[/math]


Explanation:

Question #16 (ID: 311553)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(3 a+\frac{3}{a}\right)^{2}=9[/math] হলে-
[math]\text { i. }\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=3[/math] [math]\text { ii. } a+\frac{1}{a}=1[/math] [math]\text { iii. } a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=-1[/math]
নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও ii i
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: C.ii ও iii

Solution:


Explanation:
সঠিক নয়। কারণ, [math]\left(3 a+\frac{3}{a}\right)^{2}=9[/math]
বা, [math]\left\{3\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)\right\}^{2}=9[/math]
বা, [math]9\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=9 \therefore\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=1[/math]

Question #17 (ID: 311554)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sqrt{2}[/math] এর ঘন কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]
গ. [math]3 \sqrt{2}[/math]
ঘ. 8


Correct Answer: B.[math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]

Solution:
এখানে [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
 এর ঘন নির্ণয় করার জন্য [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
 কে তিনবার গুণ করতে হবে।অর্থাৎ, [math](\sqrt{2})^{3}=\sqrt{2} \times \sqrt{2} \times \sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #18 (ID: 311555)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]4x-3=5[/math] হলে, [math]64x ^ 3 - 27 - 180x =[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. 25
খ. 125
গ. 140
ঘ. 305


Correct Answer: B.125

Solution:
ধাপ ১: প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ থেকে x-এর মান নির্ণয় করা যাক।[math]\begin{array}{l}4 x-3=5 \\4 x=5+3 \\4 x=8 \\x=\frac{8}{4} \\x=2\end{array}[/math]
ধাপ ২: এখন, প্রদত্ত রাশিটির মান নির্ণয় করা যাক।[math]64 x^{3}-27-180 x[/math]
 [math]x=2[/math]
 বসালে,[math]\begin{array}{l}=64(2)^{3}-27-180(2) \\=64 \times 8-27-360 \\=512-27-360 \\=512-387 \\=125\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #19 (ID: 311556)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a + b = 4[/math] এবং [math]a - b = 2[/math] হলে [math]a ^ 3 - b ^ 3 =[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. [math]27[/math]
খ. [math]26[/math]
গ. [math]8[/math]
ঘ. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]a+b+a-b=2+4[/math]
বা, [math]2 a=6 \quad \therefore a=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore b=4-a=4-3=1[/math]

Question #20 (ID: 311557)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p^{3}-q^{3}=45, p-q=3[/math] হলে, [math]pq=[/math]কত?

Options:
A. [math]-2[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]4[/math]
D. [math]6[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]p^{3}-q^{3}=(p-q)^{3}+3 p q(p-q)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 45=3^{3}+3 \cdot p q \cdot 3 \Rightarrow 9 p q=45-27 \Rightarrow p q=\frac{18}{9}=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x - y = 5[/math] এবং [math]xy = 6[/math] [math]x^{3}-y^{3}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 35
খ. 65
গ. 183
ঘ. 215


Correct Answer: D.215

Solution:

 [math]=5^{3}+3.6 \cdot 5=125+90=215[/math]

Question #24 (ID: 311561)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x - y = 5[/math] এবং [math]xy = 6[/math] [math]x ^ 2 - y ^ 2[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 37
খ. 35
গ. 25
ঘ. 5


Correct Answer: B.35

Solution:
[math](x+y)^{2}=(x-y)^{2}+4 x y=5^{2}+4.6=25+24=49[/math]
 [math]\therefore x+y=\sqrt{49}=7[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{2}-y^{2}=(x+y)(x-y)=7 \times 5=35[/math]


Explanation:

গ. 11
ঘ. 13

নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও :

Options:
ক. 18
খ. 36
গ. 24
ঘ. 0


Correct Answer: A.18

Solution:
[math]a^{3}+\frac{1}{a}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)=3^{3}-3.3=27-9=18[/math]

Question #29 (ID: 311566)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p+\frac{1}{p}=[/math] হলে, [math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^{2}[/math] = কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^{2}=\left(p+\frac{1}{p}\right)^{2}-4 \cdot p ; \frac{1}{p}=(2)^{2}-4=0[/math]

Explanation:

Question #30 (ID: 311567)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=2[/math] হলে, [math]x-\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-2[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
ধরি, [math]x-\frac{1}{x}=a[/math]
উভয় পক্ষে বর্গ করে পাই,[math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}-2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}-2=a^{2}[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=2[/math]
সুতরাং [math]2-2=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]0=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]a=\sqrt{0}[/math]
বা, [math]a=0[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\text { i. } p^{2}-q^{2}=7 \sqrt{41}[/math] [math]\text { ii, } p^{2}+q^{2}=45[/math] [math]\text { iii. } p^{3}-q^{3}=45 \sqrt{41}[/math]

A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: A.i ও ii

Solution:


Explanation:

 [math]\therefore p-q=\sqrt{41}[/math]
 [math]\therefore p^{3}-q^{3}=(p-q)^{3}+3 p q(p-q)=(\sqrt{41})^{3}+3.2(\sqrt{41})^{2}[/math]
 [math]=41 \sqrt{41}+6 \sqrt{41}=47 \sqrt{41} .[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 (iii) নং তথ্যটি সঠিক নয়।

Question:
[math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=1[/math] হলে [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:
আমরা জানি,[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+2 \times x \times \frac{1}{x}+\left(\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2[/math]
 [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=1[/math]
 সমীকরণে বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=1+2[/math]
 [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=3[/math]
 [math]x+\frac{1}{x}= \ \sqrt{3}[/math]
সুতরাং [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math]
 এর মান 3

Question #54 (ID: 311591)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x^{2}-4 x+1=0[/math] [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 0
খ. 2√ 3
গ. 12
ঘ. 20


Correct Answer: C.12

Solution:
[math]x^{2}+1=4 x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{x^{2}}{x}+\frac{1}{x}=\frac{4 x}{x}[/math]
বা, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math]
বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=4^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}+4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=16[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=12[/math]


Explanation:

Question #55 (ID: 311592)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x^{2}-4 x+1=0[/math] [math]x^{4}+\frac{1}{x^{4}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. 7
খ. 9
গ. 34
ঘ. 194


Correct Answer: D.194

Solution:
[math]x^{4}+\frac{1}{x^{4}}=\left(x^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}=\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x^{2} \cdot \frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\left\{\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\right\}^{2}-2=\left(4^{2}-2\right)^{2}-2=194[/math]

B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1[/math]

Solution:
[math]a^{3}-b^{3}=36[/math]
বা, [math](a-b)^{3}+3 a b(a-b)=36[/math]
বা, [math]3^{3}+3 \cdot a b \cdot 3=36[/math]
বা, [math]9 a b=36-27=9 \therefore a b=1[/math]

 এবং [math]b=2y[/math]

Question #70 (ID: 311607)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]25 \mathrm{a}^{2}+20 \mathrm{a}+\frac{1}{4 \mathrm{a}^{2}}[/math]
B. [math]5 a^{2}+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]25 \mathrm{a}^{2}+\frac{1}{4 \mathrm{a}^{2}}+5[/math]
D. [math]10 a^{2}+10 a b+\frac{1}{4 b^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]25 \mathrm{a}^{2}+\frac{1}{4 \mathrm{a}^{2}}+5[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}[/math]
 এর মান নির্ণয় করতে, আমরা [math](a+b)^{2}=a^{2}+2 a b+b^{2}[/math]
 সূত্রটি ব্যবহার করতে পারি।এখানে, [math]a=5a[/math]
 এবং [math]b=\frac{1}{2 a}[/math]
সুতরাং,[math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}=(5 a)^{2}+2 \times 5 a \times \frac{1}{2 a}+\left(\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=25 a^{2}+2 \times 5 a \times \frac{1}{2 a}+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=25 a^{2}+5+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]
অতএব [math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}=25 a^{2}+5+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]2 x+\frac{2}{x}=4[/math] হলে, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]6[/math]
D. [math]8[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]2 x+\frac{2}{x}=4[/math]
বা, [math]2\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=4[/math]
বা, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=2[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=2^{2}-2=2[/math]

বা, [math]m^{2}-2+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=36[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=36+2[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=38[/math]
সুতরাং [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}[/math]
 এর মান হবে 38

গ. 27
ঘ. 45


Correct Answer: A.9

Solution:
আমরা জানি, [math](p+q)^{3}=p^{3}+q^{3}+3 p q(p+q)[/math]
 [math]p^{3}+q^{3}=(p+q)^{3}-3 p q(p+q)[/math]
এখন, [math]p+q[/math]
 এবং [math]pq[/math]
 এর মান বসিয়ে পাই,[math]p^{3}+q^{3}=(3)^{3}-3 \times 2 \times 3[/math]
 [math]=27-18[/math]
 [math]= 09[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]a + b = 7[/math] এবং [math]ab = 10[/math]ও [math]a>b.[/math] [math]a³-b³[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 57
খ. 39
গ. 117
ঘ. 133


Correct Answer: C.117

Solution:
[math](a-b)^{2}=(a+b)^{2}-4 a b=7^{2}-4.10=9 \therefore a-b=3[/math]
সুতরাং, [math]a^{3}-b^{3}=(a-b)^{3}+3 a b(a-b)[/math]
 [math]=3^{3}+3 \cdot 10 \cdot 3=27+90=117[/math]

Question #92 (ID: 311629)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2014 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]8 x^{3}-y^{3}[/math] এর সঠিক উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]
খ. [math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}-2 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]
গ. [math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+4 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math](8 x-y)\left(64 x^{2}+8 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]

Solution:
[math]8 x^{3}-y^{3}[/math]
 এর সঠিক উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ করতে হলে আমাদের [math]a^{3}-b^{3}[/math]
 এর সূত্রটি ব্যবহার করতে হবে। সূত্রটি হলো:[math]a^{3}-b^{3}=(a-b)\left(a^{2}+a b+b^{2}\right)[/math]
এখন [math]8 x^{3}-y^{3}[/math]
 কে আমরা [math](2 x)^{3}-y^{3}[/math]
হিসেবে লিখতে পারি।এখানে, এখানে, [math]a=2x[/math]
 এবং [math]b=y[/math]
সুতরাং, আমরা সূত্রটি প্রয়োগ করলে পাই:[math]\begin{array}{l}(2 x)^{3}-y^{3}=(2 x-y)\left((2 x)^{2}+(2 x)(y)+y^{2}\right) \\=(2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #107 (ID: 311340)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^{2}-3 a-1=0[/math] হলে, [math]a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]5[/math]
খ. [math]7[/math]
গ. [math]11[/math]
ঘ. [math]13[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]11[/math]

Solution:
[math]a^{2}-3 a-1=0[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}-1=3 a[/math]
বা, [math]a-\frac{1}{a}=3[/math]
বা, [math]\left(a-\frac{i}{a}\right)^{2}=3^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]a^{2}-2 a \cdot \frac{1}{a}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=9 \quad \therefore a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=11[/math]


Explanation:

[math]\left(3 a+\frac{3}{a}\right)^{2}=9[/math] হলে-
[math]\text { i. }\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=3[/math] [math]\text { ii. } a+\frac{1}{a}=1[/math] [math]\text { iii. } a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=-1[/math]
নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

A. i ও ii

C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: C.ii ও iii

বা, [math]\left\{3\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)\right\}^{2}=9[/math]
বা, [math]9\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=9 \therefore\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=1[/math]

গ. [math]3 \sqrt{2}[/math]
ঘ. 8


Correct Answer: B.[math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]

Solution:

 এর ঘন নির্ণয় করার জন্য [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
 কে তিনবার গুণ করতে হবে।অর্থাৎ, [math](\sqrt{2})^{3}=\sqrt{2} \times \sqrt{2} \times \sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{2}[/math]

Question:
[math]4x-3=5[/math] হলে, [math]64x ^ 3 - 27 - 180x =[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. 25
খ. 125
গ. 140
ঘ. 305


Correct Answer: B.125

Solution:
ধাপ ১: প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ থেকে x-এর মান নির্ণয় করা যাক।[math]\begin{array}{l}4 x-3=5 \\4 x=5+3 \\4 x=8 \\x=\frac{8}{4} \\x=2\end{array}[/math]
ধাপ ২: এখন, প্রদত্ত রাশিটির মান নির্ণয় করা যাক।[math]64 x^{3}-27-180 x[/math]
 [math]x=2[/math]
 বসালে,[math]\begin{array}{l}=64(2)^{3}-27-180(2) \\=64 \times 8-27-360 \\=512-27-360 \\=512-387 \\=125\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Options:
ক. 37
খ. 35
গ. 25
ঘ. 5


Correct Answer: B.35

Solution:

 [math]\therefore x+y=\sqrt{49}=7[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{2}-y^{2}=(x+y)(x-y)=7 \times 5=35[/math]

Question #123 (ID: 311356)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=2[/math] হলে, [math]x-\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-2[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]4[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
ধরি, [math]x-\frac{1}{x}=a[/math]
উভয় পক্ষে বর্গ করে পাই,[math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}-2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}-2=a^{2}[/math]
প্রশ্নমতে, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=2[/math]
সুতরাং [math]2-2=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]0=a^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]a=\sqrt{0}[/math]
বা, [math]a=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]p + q = 7[/math] এবং [math]pq = 2[/math] হলে-
[math]\text { i. } p^{2}-q^{2}=7 \sqrt{41}[/math] [math]\text { ii, } p^{2}+q^{2}=45[/math] [math]\text { iii. } p^{3}-q^{3}=45 \sqrt{41}[/math]
নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও iii
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: A.i ও ii

Solution:


Explanation:
[math](p-q)^{2}=(p+q)^{2}-4 p q=(7)^{2}-4.2=49-8=41[/math]
 [math]\therefore p-q=\sqrt{41}[/math]
 [math]\therefore p^{3}-q^{3}=(p-q)^{3}+3 p q(p-q)=(\sqrt{41})^{3}+3.2(\sqrt{41})^{2}[/math]
 [math]=41 \sqrt{41}+6 \sqrt{41}=47 \sqrt{41} .[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 (iii) নং তথ্যটি সঠিক নয়।

ঘ. 35

 এবং [math]x-y=1 \ldots . . . \text { (ii) }[/math]
(i) ও (ii) যোগ করে পাই [math]2 x=6 \therefore x=3[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 (i) নং হতে, [math]y = 5 - 3 = 2[/math]
 [math]\because x^{3}-y^{3}=3^{3}-2^{3}=27-8=19[/math]

Question #134 (ID: 311367)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2018 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]2x + y = 3 xy = 1[/math] [math]4x² + y²[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 5
খ. 7
গ. 11
ঘ. 13


Correct Answer: A.5

Solution:
[math](2 x+y)=3[/math]
বা, [math](2 x+y)^{2}=3^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]4 x^{2}+4 x y+y^{2}=9[/math]
বা, [math]4 x^{2}+4.1+y^{2}=9[\because x y=1][/math]
বা, [math]\therefore 4 x^{2}+y^{2}=5[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]2x + y = 3 xy = 1[/math] [math]8 x^{3}+y^{3}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 9
খ. 18
গ. 36
ঘ. 45


Correct Answer: A.9

Solution:
[math]8 x^{3}+y^{3}=(2 x)^{3}+y^{3}=(2 x+y)^{3}-3.2 x \cdot y(2 x+y)[/math]
 [math]=3^{3}-6 \cdot 1,3=27-18=9[/math]

Question:
[math](3 x+1)(3 x-4)=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]9 x^{2}-9 x-4[/math]
B. [math]9 x^{2}+9 x-4[/math]
C. [math]9 x^{2}-9 x+4[/math]
D. [math]9 x^{2}+9 x+4[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]9 x^{2}-9 x-4[/math]

Solution:
[math](3 x+1)(3 x-4)=(3 x)^{2}+(1-4) 3 x+1 \times(-4)=9 x^{2}-9 x-4[/math]

Question #138 (ID: 311371)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=1[/math] হলে [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
C. [math]2[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\sqrt{3}[/math]

Solution:
আমরা জানি,[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+2 \times x \times \frac{1}{x}+\left(\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+2+\frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2[/math]
 [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=1[/math]
 সমীকরণে বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=1+2[/math]
 [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=3[/math]
 [math]x+\frac{1}{x}= \ \sqrt{3}[/math]
সুতরাং [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math]
 এর মান 3

Explanation:

Question #139 (ID: 311372)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x-\frac{1}{x}=6[/math] হলে, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]32[/math]
B. [math]38[/math]
C. [math]40[/math]
D. [math]44[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]40[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}+4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=(6)^{2}+4=36+4=40[/math]

Question #140 (ID: 311373)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a+\frac{1}{a}=4[/math] হলে, [math]\left(a-\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]8[/math]
B. [math]12[/math]
C. [math]16[/math]
D. [math]20[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]12[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(a-\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}-4 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}=4^{2}-4=12[/math]

Question:
[math]a^{4}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=119[/math] হলে, [math]a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]11[/math]
B. [math]\sqrt{119}[/math]
C. [math]13[/math]
D. [math]19[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]11[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(a^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(\frac{1}{a^{2}}\right)^{2}=119[/math]
বা, [math]\left(a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot a^{2} \cdot \frac{1}{a^{2}}=119[/math]
বা, [math]\left(a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}\right)^{2}=121 \therefore a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=11^{\prime}[/math]

Question:
[math]a + b = 7[/math] এবং [math]a - b = 3[/math] হলে, [math]a^{2}+b^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]20[/math]
খ. [math]29[/math]
গ. [math]40[/math]
ঘ. [math]58[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]29[/math]

Solution:
[math](a+b)^{2}=a^{2}+2 a b+b^{2}=49[/math]
 [math](a-b)^{2}=a^{2}-2 a b+b^{2}=9[/math]
সমীকরণ দুটি যোগ করে [math]2\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)=58[/math]
 [math]a^{2}+b^{2}=29[/math]


Explanation:

Question #143 (ID: 311376)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math](y + 4)(y + 2)[/math] কে দুইটি রাশির বর্গের অন্তর রূপে প্রকাশ করলে নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. [math](y + 3) ^ 2 - 1[/math]
খ. [math](y + 4) ^ 2 - 1[/math]
গ. [math](y + 2) ^ 2 - 1[/math]
ঘ. [math](x - 3) ^ 2 - 1[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math](y + 3) ^ 2 - 1[/math]

Solution:
[math](y+4)(y+2)=\left(\frac{y+4+y+2}{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{y+4-y-2}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{2 y+6}{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{2}{2}\right)^{2}=(y+3)^{2}-1^{2}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #144 (ID: 311377)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]y^{2}-2 y+1=0[/math] হলে-
[math]\text { i. } \quad\left(y-\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}=0[/math] [math]\text { ii. } y^{2}+\frac{1}{y^{2}}=2[/math] [math]\text { iii. } y^{3}-\frac{1}{y^{3}}=3[/math]
নিচের সঠিক?

Options:
A. i ও ii
B. i ও ii i
C. ii ও iii
D. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: A.i ও ii

Solution:
[math]y^{2}-2 y+1=0[/math]
বা, [math](y-1)^{2}=0[/math]
বা, [math]y-1=0 \therefore y=1[/math]
 [math]\text { (i) }\left(y-\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}=\left(1-\frac{1}{1}\right)^{2}=0 ; \text { (ii) } y^{2}+\frac{1}{y^{2}}=1^{2}+\frac{1}{1^{2}}=2[/math]
 [math]\text { (iii) } y^{3}-\frac{1}{y^{3}}=1^{3}-\frac{1}{1^{3}}=0 \text {; }[/math]
 সুতরাং, (iii) সঠিক নয়।'

Explanation:

Question #147 (ID: 311380)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x^{2}-4 x+1=0[/math] [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 0
খ. 2√ 3
গ. 12
ঘ. 20


Correct Answer: C.12

Solution:
[math]x^{2}+1=4 x[/math]
বা, [math]\frac{x^{2}}{x}+\frac{1}{x}=\frac{4 x}{x}[/math]
বা, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math]
বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=4^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}+4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=16[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=12[/math]


Explanation:

Question #148 (ID: 311381)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x^{2}-4 x+1=0[/math] [math]x^{4}+\frac{1}{x^{4}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. 7
খ. 9
গ. 34
ঘ. 194


Correct Answer: D.194

Solution:
[math]x^{4}+\frac{1}{x^{4}}=\left(x^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}=\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x^{2} \cdot \frac{1}{x^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\left\{\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\right\}^{2}-2=\left(4^{2}-2\right)^{2}-2=194[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]a^{3}-b^{3}=36, a-b=3[/math] হলে, [math]ab =[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]-1[/math]
B. [math]0[/math]
C. [math]1[/math]
D. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1[/math]

Solution:
[math]a^{3}-b^{3}=36[/math]
বা, [math](a-b)^{3}+3 a b(a-b)=36[/math]
বা, [math]3^{3}+3 \cdot a b \cdot 3=36[/math]
বা, [math]9 a b=36-27=9 \therefore a b=1[/math]

ঘ. [math]14[/math]

ক. 448
খ. 504
গ. 550
ঘ. 848

 [math]=(2 x-2)\left\{(2 x)^{2}+2.2 x+(2)^{2}\right\}[/math]
 [math]=(2 x)^{3}-2^{3}=(2.4)^{3}-8=512-8=504[/math]

Question #161 (ID: 311394)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x + 2y[/math] এর বর্গ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}[/math]
খ. [math]x^{2}+4 x y+4 y^{2}[/math]
গ. [math]x^{2}+2 x y+4 y^{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]x^{2}+x y+y^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]x^{2}+4 x y+4 y^{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]x+2y[/math]
 এর বর্গ হলো [math](x+2y)^3[/math]
এটি বের করার জন্য আমরা [math](a+b)^{2}=a^{2}+2 a b+b^{2}[/math]
 সূত্রটি ব্যবহার করতে পারি।এখানে, [math]a=x[/math]
 এবং [math]b=2y[/math]
।সুতরাং,[math]\begin{array}{l}(x+2 y)^{2}=x^{2}+2(x)(2 y)+(2 y)^{2} \\=x^{2}+4 x y+4 y^{2}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #163 (ID: 311396)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]25 \mathrm{a}^{2}+20 \mathrm{a}+\frac{1}{4 \mathrm{a}^{2}}[/math]
B. [math]5 a^{2}+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]
C. [math]25 \mathrm{a}^{2}+\frac{1}{4 \mathrm{a}^{2}}+5[/math]
D. [math]10 a^{2}+10 a b+\frac{1}{4 b^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]25 \mathrm{a}^{2}+\frac{1}{4 \mathrm{a}^{2}}+5[/math]

Solution:
[math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}[/math]
 এর মান নির্ণয় করতে, আমরা [math](a+b)^{2}=a^{2}+2 a b+b^{2}[/math]
 সূত্রটি ব্যবহার করতে পারি।এখানে, [math]a=5a[/math]
 এবং [math]b=\frac{1}{2 a}[/math]
সুতরাং,[math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}=(5 a)^{2}+2 \times 5 a \times \frac{1}{2 a}+\left(\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=25 a^{2}+2 \times 5 a \times \frac{1}{2 a}+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=25 a^{2}+5+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]
অতএব [math]\left(5 a+\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^{2}=25 a^{2}+5+\frac{1}{4 a^{2}}[/math]


Explanation:

 [math]=x(x-8)+11(x-8)[/math]
 [math]=x^{2}-8 x+11 x-88[/math]
 [math]=x^{2}+3 x-88[/math]

Question:
[math](a+13)[/math] ও [math](a-11)[/math] এর গুণফল নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]a^{2}-2 a+143[/math]
খ. [math]a^{2}+2 a-143[/math]
গ. [math]a^{2}-24 a+143[/math]
ঘ. [math]a^{2}+24 a-143[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]a^{2}+2 a-143[/math]

Solution:
গুণফলের পদ্ধতি নিচে দেওয়া হলো:[math]\begin{array}{l}(a+13)(a-11) \\=a(a-11)+13(a-11) \\=a^{2}-11 a+13 a-143 \\=a^{2}+2 a-143\end{array}[/math]

Question #166 (ID: 311399)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016, 2016 | Boards: Barisal Board, Sylhet Board | Tags: Barisal Board, Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2 x+\frac{2}{x}=4[/math] হলে, [math]x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. [math]2[/math]
C. [math]6[/math]
D. [math]8[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]2[/math]

Solution:
[math]2 x+\frac{2}{x}=4[/math]
বা, [math]2\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=4[/math]
বা, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=2[/math]
 [math]\therefore x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=2^{2}-2=2[/math]


Explanation:

Question #167 (ID: 311400)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]m-\frac{1}{m}=6[/math] হলে, [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}[/math] এর মান কত

Options:
A. [math]32[/math]
B. [math]34[/math]
C. [math]38[/math]
D. [math]40[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]38[/math]

Solution:
ধরি, [math]m-\frac{1}{m}=6[/math]
উভয়পক্ষকে বর্গ করে পাই,[math]\left(m-\frac{1}{m}\right)^{2}=6^{2}[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}-2 \times m \times \frac{1}{m}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=36[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}-2+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=36[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=36+2[/math]
বা, [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}=38[/math]
সুতরাং [math]m^{2}+\frac{1}{m^{2}}[/math]
 এর মান হবে 38

Explanation:

 [math]=\left\{\frac{2(x+5)}{2}\right\}^{2} \tau(1)^{2}=(x+5)^{2}-(1)^{2}[/math]

Question:
[math]p+q=3, p q=2[/math] হলে, [math]p^{3}+q^{3}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 9
খ. 18
গ. 27
ঘ. 45


Correct Answer: A.9

Solution:
আমরা জানি, [math](p+q)^{3}=p^{3}+q^{3}+3 p q(p+q)[/math]
 [math]p^{3}+q^{3}=(p+q)^{3}-3 p q(p+q)[/math]
এখন, [math]p+q[/math]
 এবং [math]pq[/math]
 এর মান বসিয়ে পাই,[math]p^{3}+q^{3}=(3)^{3}-3 \times 2 \times 3[/math]
 [math]=27-18[/math]
 [math]= 09[/math]

নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]a + b = 7[/math] এবং [math]ab = 10[/math]ও [math]a>b.[/math] [math]a³-b³[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 57
খ. 39
গ. 117
ঘ. 133


Correct Answer: C.117

Solution:
[math](a-b)^{2}=(a+b)^{2}-4 a b=7^{2}-4.10=9 \therefore a-b=3[/math]
সুতরাং, [math]a^{3}-b^{3}=(a-b)^{3}+3 a b(a-b)[/math]
 [math]=3^{3}+3 \cdot 10 \cdot 3=27+90=117[/math]

Question:
[math]8 x^{3}-y^{3}[/math] এর সঠিক উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]
খ. [math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}-2 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]
গ. [math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+4 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math](8 x-y)\left(64 x^{2}+8 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math](2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}\right)[/math]

Solution:
[math]8 x^{3}-y^{3}[/math]
 এর সঠিক উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ করতে হলে আমাদের [math]a^{3}-b^{3}[/math]
 এর সূত্রটি ব্যবহার করতে হবে। সূত্রটি হলো:[math]a^{3}-b^{3}=(a-b)\left(a^{2}+a b+b^{2}\right)[/math]
এখন [math]8 x^{3}-y^{3}[/math]
 কে আমরা [math](2 x)^{3}-y^{3}[/math]
হিসেবে লিখতে পারি।এখানে, এখানে, [math]a=2x[/math]
 এবং [math]b=y[/math]
সুতরাং, আমরা সূত্রটি প্রয়োগ করলে পাই:[math]\begin{array}{l}(2 x)^{3}-y^{3}=(2 x-y)\left((2 x)^{2}+(2 x)(y)+y^{2}\right) \\=(2 x-y)\left(4 x^{2}+2 x y+y^{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:

Options:
ক. 11
খ. [math]\sqrt{119}[/math]
গ. 13
ঘ. 19


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:

গ. 12
ঘ. 20

Solution:

Question #193 (ID: 801784)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: আদমজী ক্যান্টনমেন্ট পাবলিক স্কুল, ঢাকা
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+y=\sqrt{3}, x y=1 \text { হলে } x^3+y^3=\text { কত ? }[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]3 \sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]1[/math]
ঘ. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; x^3+y^3=(x+y)^3-3 x y(x+y)\\&amp;=(\sqrt{3})^3-3 \times 1 \times \sqrt{3} \\&amp; =3 \sqrt{3}-3 \sqrt{3}=0\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii

Question:

[math]x^4+\frac{1}{x^4}=\text { কত?}[/math]

Options:
ক. 7
খ. 9
গ. 34
ঘ. 194


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}x^4 &amp; +\frac{1}{x^4}=\left(x^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^2\\&amp;=\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^2-2 \cdot x^2 \cdot \frac{1}{x^2} \\&amp; =\left\{\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\right\}^2-2\\&amp;=\left(4^2-2\right)^2-2=194\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #215 (ID: 801806)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: রা. বো.'২০১৭;রা. বো.'২০১৬
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=2[/math] হয় তাহলে [math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
খ. 2
গ. 12
ঘ. 14


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^3-3 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math][math]=2^3-3 \times 2=2[/math]

Explanation:

Question #225 (ID: 801816)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ঢা. বো.'২০১৭

Question:
[math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=1[/math] হলে [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]2[/math]
ঘ. [math]3[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
এখানে, [math]\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=1+2[/math][math]\therefore x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}[/math]

ক. [math]\sqrt{29}[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{27}[/math]

ঘ. [math]\sqrt{21}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:

Correct Answer: গ

eq 0[/math]

Question #241 (ID: 801832)

Question:
[math]x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে [math]x^4+x^2+1[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 8
খ. [math]2 x^2[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm{x}^2[/math]
ঘ. [math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{2}[/math] বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=2[/math]বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}+2=2[/math] বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=0[/math] বা, [math]x^4+1=0 \therefore x^4=-1[/math]এখন, [math]x^4+x^2+1=-1+x^2+1=x^2[/math]

Question #247 (ID: 801838)

Question:
যদি [math]\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}=-\mathrm{z}[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\mathrm{x}^3+\mathrm{y}^3+\mathrm{z}^3-3 \mathrm{xyz}[/math] এর মান কত? 

Options:
ক. [math]1[/math]
খ. [math]0[/math]
গ. [math]x^2+z^2[/math]
ঘ. [math]6 x y z+2 z^3[/math]

Question #249 (ID: 801840)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags:

Question:
[math]x^2+\sqrt{3} x+1=0[/math]

[math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
খ. [math]6 \sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]3 \sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]6 \sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:


Explanation:

Question #250 (ID: 801841)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{x}^2=5+2 \sqrt{6}[/math] 

[math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]
গ. [math]3 \sqrt{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]3 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2} \text { বা, } \frac{1}{x}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}}{(\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2})(\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2})}[/math]বা, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}}{(\sqrt{3})^2-(\sqrt{2})^2} \therefore \frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}[/math][math]\therefore x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}+\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #276 (ID: 801717)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a ^ 2 - b ^ 2 = 2[/math], [math]a-b= 1[/math] হলে, [math]a + b[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 1
খ. 2
গ. 3
ঘ. 4


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \text { } a^2-b^2=(a+b)(a-b) \\ &amp; \text { বा, } 2=(a+b) \times 1 \therefore a+b=2\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #277 (ID: 801718)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathbf{m}+\frac{1}{\mathbf{m}}=2[/math] হলে [math]\mathbf{m}^4+\frac{1}{\mathbf{m}^4}=[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 1
খ. 2
গ. 3
ঘ. 4


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{m}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}^4}=\left(\mathrm{m}^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}^2}\right)^2[/math][math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =\left(\mathrm{m}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}^2}\right)^2-2 \times \mathrm{m}^2 \times \frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}^2} \\ &amp; =\left\{\left(\mathrm{m}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}}\right)^2-2 \times \mathrm{m} \times \frac{1}{\mathrm{~m}}\right\}^2-2 \\ &amp; =\left\{(2)^2-2\right\}^2-2 \\ &amp; =(4-2)^2-2=4-2=2\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]p = b - 2c, q = a + 3c[/math] হলে [math](p + q) ^ 2[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]a ^ 2 + 2ab + b ^ 2 [/math]
খ. [math]b ^ 2 - 4bc + c ^ 2 [/math]
গ. [math]a ^ 2 + 6c + 9c ^ 2 [/math]
ঘ. [math]a ^ 2 + b ^ 2 + c ^ 2 + 2ab + 2bc + 2ca[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
ঘ. [math]a ^ 2 + b ^ 2 + c ^ 2 + 2ab + 2bc + 2ca[/math]

Question #288 (ID: 801729)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a+b=11[/math] এবং [math]a- b = 3[/math] হলে [math]ab =[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. 130
খ. 260
গ. 28
ঘ. 56


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]a b=\left(\frac{a+b}{2}\right)^2-\left(\frac{a-b}{2}\right)^2=\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^2-\left(\frac{3}{2}\right)^2\\=\frac{121}{4}-\frac{9}{4}=\frac{121-9}{4}=\frac{112}{4}=28[/math]

Explanation:

Question #332 (ID: 801773)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: চ. বো.'২০১৬
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a+b-c[/math] এই বীজগণিতীয় রাশির বর্গ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]a^2+b^2+c^2[/math]
খ. [math]a^2+b^2-c^2+2 a b-2 b c-2 c a[/math]
গ. [math]a^2+b^2+c^2-2 a b-2 b c-2 c a[/math]
ঘ. [math]a^2+b^2+c^2+2 a b-2 b c-2 c a[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math](a+b-c)^2=a^2+b^2+(-c)^2[/math][math]+2 a b+2 \cdot b \cdot(-c)+2(-c) \cdot a \\=a^2+b^2+c^2+2 a b-2 b c-2 c a .[/math]

Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
p + q = 7 এবং pq = 9 হলে, p² + q² এর মান কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 67
খ. 40
গ. 31
ঘ. 13


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]p^2+q^2=(p+q)^2-2 p q[/math][math]=7^2-2 \times 9=49-18=31[/math]

Explanation:

Question:

Options:
ক. 16
খ. 26
গ. 46
ঘ. 56

Question #347 (ID: 801604)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x ^ 2 - y ^ 2, x + y, x ^ 3  y + x ^ 2  y ^ 2[/math] তিনটি রাশি।

১ম ও ২য় রাশির ল. সা. গু. নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]x + y [/math]
খ. [math]x - y [/math]
গ. [math]x ^ 2 - y ^ 2 [/math]
ঘ. [math](x + y) ^ 2 [/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
১ম রাশি, [math]x^2-y^2=(x+y)(x-y)[/math]২য় রাশি [math]=x+y[/math]নির্ণেয় ল. সা. গু. [math]=(x+y)(x-y)=x^2-y^2[/math]

Explanation:

Question #351 (ID: 801608)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math](x²+ y²)²[/math] এবং [math](x^4 + y^4)[/math] এর গ. সা. গু. কত?

Options:
ক. [math]x+y [/math]
খ. [math]x&sup2; + y&sup2; [/math]
গ. [math]x&sup2; - y&sup2;[/math]
ঘ. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
১ম রাশি [math]\left(x^2+y^2\right)^2=\left(x^2+y^2\right)\left(x^2+y^2\right)[/math]২য় রাশি [math]\left(x^4+y^4\right)=\left(x^2\right)^2+\left(y^2\right)^2[/math][math]=\left(x^2+y^2\right)^2-2 x^2 y^2[/math]নিণেয় গ. সা. গু.।

Explanation:

Question #359 (ID: 801616)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: রা. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x ^ 2 - 5x, x ^ 2 - 25[/math] এবং [math]x ^ 2 - 7x + 10[/math] এর গ.সা.গু. কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]x[/math]
খ. [math]x - 5[/math]
গ. [math]x - 2[/math]
ঘ. [math]x + 5[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \text { প্রথম রাশি }=x(x-5) \\ &amp; \text { দ্বিতীয় রাশি }=(x+5)(x-5) \\ &amp; \text { তৃতীয় রাশি }=x^2-5 x-2 x+10 \\ &amp; \quad=x(x-5)-2(x-5)=(x-5)(x-2) \\ &amp; \therefore \text { নির্ণেয় গ.সা.গু }=x-5\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

Question #360 (ID: 801617)

Question #365 (ID: 801622)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]3(a+b), 9\left(a^2-b^2\right)[/math] ও [math]18\left(a^3+b^3\right)[/math] এর গ. সা. গু কত?

Options:
ক. [math]a+b[/math]
খ. [math]3(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})[/math]
গ. [math](a-b)\left(a^3+b^3\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]18(a-b)\left(a^3+b^3\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
প্রথম রাশি [math]=3(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})[/math]দ্বিতীয় রাশি [math]=9\left(\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{b}^2\right)=3.3(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})[/math]তৃতীয় রাশি [math]=18\left(\mathrm{a}^3+\mathrm{b}^3\right)=6.3 .(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})\left(\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{ab}+\mathrm{b}^2\right)[/math][math]\therefore[/math] গ. সা. গু [math]=3(a+b)[/math]

Explanation:

Question #367 (ID: 801624)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a-b, a^2-a b, a^2-b^2[/math] এর ল.সা.গু. নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})[/math]
খ. [math]\mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm{a}\left(\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{b}^2\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math]\mathrm{a}\left(\mathrm{a}^2+\mathrm{b}^2\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
১ম রাশি = [math]a-b[/math]; ২য় রাশি = [math]a(a-b)[/math]৩য় রাশি [math]=(a+b)(a-b)[/math][math]\therefore[/math] নির্ণেয় ল.সা.গু. [math]=a(a-b)(a+b)=a\left(a^2-b^2\right)[/math]

Explanation:

Question #374 (ID: 801631)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ব. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{a}^3-\mathrm{b}^3[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{a}^3+\mathrm{b}^3[/math] এর গ. সা. গু কত?

Options:
খ. 1
গ. [math]a-b[/math]
ঘ. [math]a+b[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \mathrm{a}^3-\mathrm{b}^3=(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})\left(\mathrm{a}^2+\mathrm{ab}+\mathrm{b}^2\right) \\&amp; \mathrm{a}^3+\mathrm{b}^3=(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})\left(\mathrm{a}^2-\mathrm{ab}+\mathrm{b}^2\right) \\&amp; \therefore \text { গ. সা. গু }=1\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #377 (ID: 801634)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: দি. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2(a+b), 4\left(a^2-b^2\right)[/math] এবং [math]12\left(a^2 b+a b^2\right)[/math] তিনটি বীজগাণিতিক রাশি।

রাশি তিনটির গ.সা.গু. নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}[/math]
খ. [math]2(a+b)[/math]
গ. [math]4(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})[/math]
ঘ. [math]12(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
প্রথম রাশি [math]=2(a+b)[/math]দ্বিতীয় রাশি [math]=4\left(a^2-b^2\right)=2.2(a+b)(a-b)[/math]তৃতীয় রাশি [math]=12\left(a^2 b+a b^2\right)=2 \cdot 2 \cdot 3 \cdot a b(a+b)[/math][math]\therefore[/math] গ.সা.গু. [math]=2(a+b)[/math]

Explanation:

Question #380 (ID: 801637)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^3-2 x^2, x^2-4[/math] এবং [math]x y-2 y[/math] এর গ.সা.গু. কত? 

Options:
ক. [math]1[/math]
খ. [math]\mathrm{x}-2[/math]
গ. [math]x^2 y(x-2)[/math]
ঘ. [math]{x}^2 y\left(x^2-4\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
১ম রাশি [math]=\mathrm{x}^3-2 \mathrm{x}^2=\mathrm{x}^2(\mathrm{x}-2)[/math]২য় রাশি [math]=x^2-4=(x+2)(x-2)[/math]৩য় রাশি [math]=x y-2 y=y(x-2)[/math][math]\therefore[/math] গ.সা.গু. [math]=(x-2)[/math]

Explanation:

Question #381 (ID: 801638)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: য. বো.'২০১৭
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2 x\left(x^3-1\right), 4 x^2\left(x^2-1\right)[/math] এর গ.সা.গু. কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2 x[/math]
খ. [math]2 x(x+1)[/math]
গ. [math]2 x(x-1)[/math]
ঘ. [math]4 x^2\left(x^2-1\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
১ম রাশি [math]=2 \mathrm{x}\left(\mathrm{x}^3-1\right)=2 \mathrm{x}(\mathrm{x}-1)\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\mathrm{x}+1\right)[/math]২য় রাশি [math]=4 \mathrm{x}^2\left(\mathrm{x}^2-1\right)=4 \mathrm{x}^2(\mathrm{x}+1)(\mathrm{x}-1)[/math][math]\therefore[/math] নির্ণেয় গ. সা.গু [math]=2 \mathrm{x}(\mathrm{x}-1)[/math]

Explanation:

Question #383 (ID: 801640)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: চ. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p ^ 2 - 4p + 3[/math] এবং [math]p ^ 2 - 9[/math] দুইটি বীজগাণিতিক রাশি হলে-

i. রাশি দুইটির গ.সা.গু [math]p - 3[/math]

ii. রাশি দুইটির ল.সা.গু [math]p(p + 3)(p - 3)(p - 1)[/math]

iii. ১ম রাশিতে [math]p ^ 2[/math] এর সহগ [math]1[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. ii ও iii
গ. i ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \mathrm{p}^2-4 \mathrm{p}+3=\mathrm{p}^2-3 \mathrm{p}-\mathrm{p}+3=(\mathrm{p}-3)(\mathrm{p}-1) \\ &amp; \mathrm{p}^2-9=(\mathrm{p}+3)(\mathrm{p}-3) \\ &amp; \therefore \text { গ.সা.গু }=\mathrm{p}-3 \\ &amp; \text { এবং ল.সা.গু }=(\mathrm{p}+3)(\mathrm{p}-3)(\mathrm{p}-1)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #386 (ID: 801581)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: ময়মনসিংহ জিলা স্কুল

Question:
[math]x^3+3 \sqrt{3}[/math] এর উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](x-\sqrt{3})\left(x^2+\sqrt{3} x+3\right)[/math]
খ. [math](x+\sqrt{3})\left(x^2-\sqrt{3} x+3\right)[/math]
গ. [math](x+\sqrt{3})\left(x^2+\sqrt{3} x+3\right)[/math]

Question:
নিচের কোনটি [math]3a ^ 2 + 11a - 4[/math] এর একটি উৎপাদক? 

Options:
ক. a - 4
খ. 3a + 1
গ. 3a - 1
ঘ. a - 1


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; 3 a^2+11 a-4=3 a^2+12 a-a-4 \\ &amp; =3 a(a+4)-1(a+4)=(a+4)(3 a-1)\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #396 (ID: 801591)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: চ. বো.'২০১৭
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x ^ 4 - 2x ^ 2 + 1[/math] এর একটি উৎপাদক হলো-

Options:
ক. 2 + 1
খ. x<sup>2</sup> + 1
গ. x + 1
ঘ. 2x - 1


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} x^4- &amp; 2 x^2+1=x^4-x^2-x^2+1 \\ &amp; =x^2\left(x^2-1\right)-\left(x^2-1\right)\\&amp;=\left(x^2-1\right)\left(x^2-1\right) \\ &amp; =(x+1)(x-1)\left(x^2-1\right)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]2x ^ 2 + 7x - 4[/math] এর উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষিত রূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. (2x - 1)(x - 4)
খ. (2x + 1)(x - 4)
গ. (2x - 1)(x + 4)
ঘ. (2x + 1)(x + 4)&nbsp;


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; 2 x^2+7 x-4 \\ &amp; =2 x^2+8 x-x-4 \\ &amp; =2 x(x+4)-1(x+4) \\ &amp; =(x+4)(2 x-1)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

খ. x + 1
গ. x<sup>2</sup> + 2x + 1
ঘ. x<sup>2</sup> + x + 1


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\mathrm{x}^3+1=(\mathrm{x})^3+(1)^3=(\mathrm{x}+1)\left(\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{x}+1\right)[/math]

ক. (x + 4)(x + 3)

গ. (x - 4)(x - 3)
ঘ. (x + 4)(- x + 3)


Correct Answer: ক

Question #413 (ID: 801548)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]8x ^ 3 + 36x ^ 2 + 54x + 27[/math] একটি বীজগণিতীয় রাশি।

Options:
ক. (2x + 3)
খ. (2x - 3)
গ. (3x + 2)
ঘ. (3x - 2)


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; 8 x^3+36 x^2+54 x+27 \\ &amp; =(2 x)^3+3 \times(2 x)^2 \times 3+3 \times 2 x \times(3)^2+(3)^3 \\ &amp; =(2 x+3)^3=(2 x+3)(2 x+3)(2 x+3)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #418 (ID: 801553)

Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
2a2 + 10a + 12 রাশিটির একটি উৎপাদক-

i. a + 2 

ii. a + 4 

iii. a + 3 

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক? 

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} 2 a^2+10 a+12 &amp; =2 a^2+4 a+6 a+12 \\ &amp; =2 a(a+2)+6(a+2) \\ &amp; =(a+2)(2 a+6) \\ &amp; =2(a+2)(a+3)\end{aligned}[/math]সুতরাং। ও iii উক্তিটি সঠিক।

Question #435 (ID: 801570)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: কু. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a ^ 2 - 2ab + 2b - 1[/math] এর একটি উৎপাদক-

Options:
ক. [math](a + 1)[/math]
খ. [math](a - 1)[/math]
গ. [math](a - 2b)[/math]
ঘ. [math](a + 2b)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; a^2-1-2 a b+2 b=(a+1)(a-1)-2 b(a-1) \\ &amp; =(a-1)(a+1-2 b)=(a-1)(a-2 b+1) \end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #440 (ID: 801575)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: য. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2x ^ 2 - 7xy + 6y ^ 2[/math] এর উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষিত রূপ নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. (x - 2y)(2x - 3y)
খ. (x + 2y)(2x - 3y)
গ. (x - 2y)(2x + 3y)
ঘ. (x + 2y)(2x + 3y)


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; 2 x^2-7 x y+6 y^2 \\ &amp; =2 x^2-4 x y-3 x y+6 y^2 \\ &amp; =2 x(x-2 y)-3 y(x-2 y) \\ &amp; =(x-2 y)(2 x-3 y)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #443 (ID: 801578)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: কু. বো.'২০১৬
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x ^ 2 + 7x + 12[/math] রাশিটির-

i. x এর সহগ 7

ii. ধ্রুবক পদ 12

iii. একটি উৎপাদক x + 3

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]x^2+7 x+12[math]=x^2+3 x+4 x+12=x(x+3)+4(x+3)[/math] =(x+3)(x+4)[/math]

Explanation:

Question #444 (ID: 801579)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: দি. বো.'২০১৭
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]27a ^ 3 - 8[/math] এর উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](3a + 2)(9a ^ 2 - 6a + 4)[/math]
খ. [math](3a + 2)(9a ^ 2 + 6a + 4)[/math]
গ. [math](3a - 2)(9a ^ 2 - 6a + 4)[/math]
ঘ. [math](3a - 2)(9a ^ 2 + 6a + 4)[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; 27 a^3-8=(3 a)^3-(2)^3\\&amp;=(3 a-2)\left\{(3 a)^2+3 a \cdot 2+(2)^2\right\} \\ &amp;=(3 a-2)\left(9 a^2+6 a+4\right)\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #485 (ID: 801470)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: আদমজী ক্যান্টনমেন্ট পাবলিক স্কুল, ঢাকা
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+y=\sqrt{3}, x y=1 \text { হলে } x^3+y^3=\text { কত ? }[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]3 \sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]1[/math]
ঘ. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; x^3+y^3=(x+y)^3-3 x y(x+y)\\&amp;=(\sqrt{3})^3-3 \times 1 \times \sqrt{3} \\&amp; =3 \sqrt{3}-3 \sqrt{3}=0\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #486 (ID: 801471)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৭
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+y=6 \text { এবং } x y=5 \text { হলে- }[/math]

i. [math]x-y=4[/math]

ii. [math]x^3-y^3=124[/math]

iii. [math]x^3+y^3=130[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
(i) [math]x+y=6[/math]বা, [math](x+y)^2=36[/math] বা,[math](x-y)^2+4 x y=36[/math]বা, [math](x-y)^2=36-20 \therefore x-y=4[/math](ii) [math]x^3-y^3=(x-y)^3+3 x y(x-y)[math]=(4)^3+3.5 .4=124[/math](iii) [math]x^3+y^3=(x+y)^3-3 x y(x+y)[/math]=(6)^3-3.5 .6=126[/math][math]\therefore[/math] (iii) নং সত্য নয়।

Explanation:

Question #487 (ID: 801472)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: রা. বো.'২০১৯
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x-y=5 \text { এবং } x y=6[/math]

[math]\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{y}^2[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 37
খ. 35
গ. 25
ঘ. 5


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; (x+y)^2=(x-y)^2+4 x y\\&amp;=5^2+4.6=25+24=49 \\&amp; \therefore x+y=7 \\&amp; \therefore x^2-y^2=(x+y)(x-y)=7 \times 5=35\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

Question:
[math]2x + y = 3, xy = 1[/math]

ক. 5
খ. 7
গ. 11
ঘ. 13


Correct Answer: ক

Question #490 (ID: 801475)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: সি. বো.'২০১৮
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2x + y = 3, xy = 1[/math]

[math]8x ^ 3 + y ^ 3[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. 9
খ. 18
গ. 36
ঘ. 45


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; 8 x^3+y^3=(2 x)^3+y^3 \\ &amp; =(2 x+y)^3-3 \cdot 2 x \cdot y(2 x+y) \\ &amp; =3^3-6 \cdot 1 \cdot 3=27-18=9\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #493 (ID: 801478)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{x}^2=5+2 \sqrt{6}[/math] 

x এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{5}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; x^2=5+2 \sqrt{6}\\&amp;=(\sqrt{3})^2+2 \sqrt{3} \cdot \sqrt{2}+(\sqrt{2})^2=(\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2})^2 \\&amp; \therefore x=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}\end{aligned}[/math]

Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\\&amp;=(2 \sqrt{3})^2-4=8 \\&amp; \therefore x-\frac{1}{x}=2 \sqrt{2} \\&amp; x^3-\frac{1}{x^3}=\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^3+3 \cdot x \frac{1}{x}\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)\\&amp;=(2 \sqrt{2})^3+3 \times 2 \sqrt{2}=22 \sqrt{2}\end{aligned}[/math]

Explanation:

[math]\mathrm{x}^3+2[/math] এর ঘন নিচের কোনটি?

Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\left(x^3+2\right)^3\\=\left(x^3\right)^3 +3 \left({x}^3\right)^2 \cdot 2+3 \cdot x^3 \cdot(2)^2+(2)^3 \\=x^9+6 x^6+12 x^3+8[/math]

Question:
p3 - q3 = 45, p - q = 3 হলে, pq = কত?

Options:
ক. -2
খ. 2
গ. 4
ঘ. 6


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \mathrm{p}^3-\mathrm{q}^3=(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})^3+3 \mathrm{pq}(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q}) \\ &amp; \Rightarrow 45=3^3+3 \cdot \mathrm{pq} \cdot 3 \\&amp; \Rightarrow 9 \mathrm{pq}=45-27 \Rightarrow \mathrm{pq}=\frac{18}{9}=2\end{aligned}[/math]

Question #512 (ID: 801497)

Question:
যদি [math]\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}=-\mathrm{z}[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\mathrm{x}^3+\mathrm{y}^3+\mathrm{z}^3-3 \mathrm{xyz}[/math] এর মান কত? 

Options:
ক. [math]1[/math]
খ. [math]0[/math]

Question #515 (ID: 801500)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{x}^2=5+2 \sqrt{6}[/math] 

[math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]2 \sqrt{2}[/math]
গ. [math]3 \sqrt{2}[/math]
ঘ. [math]3 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2} \text { বা, } \frac{1}{x}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}}{(\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2})(\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2})}[/math]বা, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}}{(\sqrt{3})^2-(\sqrt{2})^2} \therefore \frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}[/math][math]\therefore x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}+\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #516 (ID: 644534)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^{8}-b^{8}[/math] এর উৎপাদক কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](a-b)(a+b)(a^{2}+b^{2})(a^{4}+b^{4})[/math]
খ. [math](a^{2}-b^{2})(a^{6}+a^{4}b^{2}+b^{6})[/math]
গ. [math](a^{4}+b^{4})(a^{4}-a^{2}b^{2}+b^{4})[/math]
ঘ. [math](a^{2}+ab+b^{2})(a^{6}-a^{5}b+a^{4}b^{2}-a^{3}b^{3}+a^{2}b^{4}-ab^{5}+b^{6})[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
প্রথমে [math]a^{8}-b^{8}[/math] কে পার্থকে ভাগ করা যায়: [math]a^{8}-b^{8}=(a^{4}-b^{4})(a^{4}+b^{4})[/math]. আবার [math]a^{4}-b^{4}=(a^{2}-b^{2})(a^{2}+b^{2})[/math] এবং [math]a^{2}-b^{2}=(a-b)(a+b)[/math]. সুতরাং সম্পূর্ণভাবে উৎপাদক হবে:
[math](a-b)(a+b)(a^{2}+b^{2})(a^{4}+b^{4}).[/math]

Explanation:
উপরের পদক্ষেপগুলোর সরলীকরণ থেকে স্পষ্ট যে [math](a-b)(a+b)(a^{2}+b^{2})(a^{4}+b^{4})[/math] হল সঠিক পূর্ণ উৎপাদক। অন্য বিকল্পগুলো যাচাই করলে তারা আসল অভিব্যক্তির সাথে মেলে না: উদাহরণস্বরূপ বিকল্প [math]খ[/math] বা [math]গ[/math] গুণ করলে অতিরিক্ত বা অনুপস্থিত ক্রস-টারের্ম দেখা যায় এবং [math]ঘ[/math] একটি ভিন্ন ধরণের বিভাজন (৭-ধারার সমষ্টি) যা [math]a^{8}-b^{8}[/math] এর সমান নয়। তাই সঠিক উত্তর হচ্ছে ক।

Question #517 (ID: 644528)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+y=\sqrt{7}[/math] এবং [math]x-y=\sqrt{3}[/math] হলে, [math]x^{3}+y^{3}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]4\sqrt{7}[/math]
খ. [math]7\sqrt{7}-3\sqrt{3}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{7}-3\sqrt{3}[/math]
ঘ. [math]5\sqrt{7}-\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x^{3}+y^{3}=(x+y)^{3}-3xy(x+y)[/math]

প্রথমে [math]xy[/math] নির্ণয় করতে হবে।
[math]4xy=(x+y)^{2}-(x-y)^{2}=(\sqrt{7})^{2}-(\sqrt{3})^{2}=7-3=4[/math]
অতএব [math]xy=1[/math]।

এখন,
[math]x^{3}+y^{3}=(\sqrt{7})^{3}-3\cdot 1\cdot \sqrt{7}=7\sqrt{7}-3\sqrt{7}=4\sqrt{7}[/math]।

Explanation:
সমীকরণগুলোর সাহায্যে [math]xy[/math] বের করার জন্য পরিচিত পরিচয় ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে: [math]4xy=(x+y)^{2}-(x-y)^{2}[/math]। তারপর [math]x^{3}+y^{3}[/math] নির্ণয়ের জন্য [math]x^{3}+y^{3}=(x+y)^{3}-3xy(x+y)[/math] সূত্র প্রয়োগ করা হয়েছে, ও সরলীকরণ করলে উত্তর [math]4\sqrt{7}[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #518 (ID: 644529)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]4x+5y=22[/math] এবং [math]xy=3[/math] হলে, [math]64x^{3}+125y^{3}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 6688
খ. 5324
গ. 7426
ঘ. 10648


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]64x^{3}+125y^{3}=(4x)^{3}+(5y)^{3}[/math]
[math]= (4x+5y)^{3}-3(4x)(5y)(4x+5y)[/math]
এখানে [math]4x+5y=22[/math] এবং [math]xy=3[/math]। তাই
[math](4x+5y)^{3}=22^{3}=10648[/math]
[math]3(4x)(5y)(4x+5y)=3\cdot 20\cdot xy\cdot 22=60\cdot 3\cdot 22=3960[/math]
অতএব [math]64x^{3}+125y^{3}=10648-3960=6688[/math].

Explanation:
সমীকরণটি দুটো ঘাতের যোগের ফর্মে আছে। [math]a^{3}+b^{3}=(a+b)^{3}-3ab(a+b)[/math] সূত্র ব্যবহার করলে সহজেই মান নির্ণয় করা যায়। এখানে [math]a=4x,\; b=5y[/math] এবং দেওয়া মানগুলি স্থাপন করলে ফলাফল [math]6688[/math] আসে।

Question #519 (ID: 644527)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math](x + 8)(x + 2)[/math] এর দুইটি রাশির বর্গের অন্তররূপ কোনটি?

Options:
ক/a/ا. [math](x+5)^{2}-(1)^{2}[/math]
খ/b/ب. [math]x^{2}-36[/math]
গ/c/ج. [math](x+7)^{2}-(1)^{2}[/math]
ঘ/d/ث. [math](x+5)^{2}-(3)^{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: ঘ/d/ث

Solution:
[math](x+8)(x+2)[/math]
[math]=\left(\frac{(x+8)+(x+2)}{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{(x+8)-(x+2)}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
[math]=\left(\frac{2x+10}{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{6}{2}\right)^{2}=(x+5)^{2}-(3)^{2}[/math]

Explanation:
দুটি রাশি [math]a[/math] ও [math]b[/math] হলে তাদের গুণকে আমরা মধ্যমান ও আধা-প্রভেদ ব্যবহার করে [math](\frac{a+b}{2})^{2}-(\frac{a-b}{2})^{2}[/math] হিসেবে লিখতে পারি। এখানে [math]a=x+8,\; b=x+2[/math] নিলে মধ্যমান [math]x+5[/math] এবং আধা-প্রভেদ [math]3[/math], অতএব ফলাফল [math](x+5)^{2}-(3)^{2}[/math]।

Question #520 (ID: 644525)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নেটির উত্তর দাও:
[math]x^{2}-4 x+1=0[/math] [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]2\sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt{5}[/math]
গ. [math]4[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{8}[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]x^{2}-4x+1=0[/math]
বা, [math]x^{2}+1=4x\Rightarrow x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math]
তাহলে, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)=\sqrt{\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-4\cdot x\frac{1}{x}}=\sqrt{4^{2}-4}=\sqrt{12}=2\sqrt{3}[/math]

Explanation:
দেওয়া সমীকরণ থেকে [math]x+\dfrac{1}{x}=4[/math] পাওয়া যায়। [math]x-\dfrac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান বের করতে যোগ ও বিয়োগ সূত্র ব্যবহার করলে [math]\left(x-\dfrac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=(x+\dfrac{1}{x})^{2}-4[/math] হয়। এখানে এটি [math]\sqrt{16-4}=\sqrt{12}=2\sqrt{3}[/math] হয়। (প্রশ্নে সাধারনত ধনাত্মক মূল নেওয়া হয়।)

Question #521 (ID: 644526)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]y^{2}+6 y+9=0[/math] হলে-
[math]\text { i. } \quad\left(y+\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}=\frac{100}{9}[/math] [math]\text { ii. } y^{2}+\frac{1}{y^{2}}=\frac{82}{9}[/math] [math]\text { iii. } y^{3}+\frac{1}{y^{3}}=-\frac{1000}{27}[/math]
নিচের সঠিক?

Options:
ক. i ও ii
খ. i ও iii
গ. ii ও iii
ঘ. i, ii ও iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]y^{2}+6y+9=0[/math]
বা, [math](y+3)^{2}=0[/math]
অতএব [math]y=-3[/math]
(i) [math]\left(y+\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}=\left(-3+\frac{1}{-3}\right)^{2}=\left(-\frac{10}{3}\right)^{2}=\frac{100}{9}[/math] — সঠিক।
(ii) [math]y^{2}+\frac{1}{y^{2}}=(-3)^{2}+\frac{1}{(-3)^{2}}=9+\frac{1}{9}=\frac{81+1}{9}=\frac{82}{9}[/math] — সঠিক।
(iii) [math]y^{3}+\frac{1}{y^{3}}=(-3)^{3}+\frac{1}{(-3)^{3}}=-27-\frac{1}{27}=\frac{-729-1}{27}= -\frac{730}{27}[/math] — দেয়া মান [math]-\frac{1000}{27}[/math] ভুল।

Explanation:
সমীকরণ থেকে [math]y=-3[/math] পাওয়া যায়। (i) ও (ii) তে প্রদত্ত মানগুলি অব্যাহতভাবে হিসাব করলে মিলে যায়; কিন্তু (iii) এর জন্য সঠিক মান [math]-\frac{730}{27}[/math], প্রদত্ত [math]-\frac{1000}{27}[/math] ভুল। সুতরাং ক (i ও ii) সঠিক।

Question #522 (ID: 644524)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x-\frac{1}{x}=2[/math] হলে, [math]x^{3}-\frac{1}{x^{3}}[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]10[/math]
খ. [math]12[/math]
গ. [math]14[/math]
ঘ. [math]16[/math]


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math](x-\frac{1}{x})^{3}=x^{3}-\frac{1}{x^{3}}-3x+\frac{3}{x}[/math] থেকে, [math]x^{3}-\frac{1}{x^{3}}=(x-\frac{1}{x})^{3}+3\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math]. এতে [math]x-\frac{1}{x}=2[/math] প্রদান করলে, [math]x^{3}-\frac{1}{x^{3}}=2^{3}+3\cdot2=8+6=14[/math].

Explanation:
বাইনোমিয়াল সম্প্রসারণ ব্যবহার করে পরিচয়টি পাওয়া যায়: [math]x^{3}-\frac{1}{x^{3}}=(x-\frac{1}{x})^{3}+3(x-\frac{1}{x})[/math]. প্রদত্ত মান বসিয়ে সহজভাবে ফলাফল [math]14[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #523 (ID: 644523)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও :
[math]x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math] [math]x^{3}+\frac{1}{x^{3}}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. 60
খ. 52
গ. 28
ঘ. 0


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text{ধরি }a= x+\frac{1}{x}=4.[/math]
[math](x+\frac{1}{x})^{3}=x^{3}+\frac{1}{x^{3}}+3\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math]
অতএব [math]x^{3}+\frac{1}{x^{3}}=(x+\frac{1}{x})^{3}-3\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=a^{3}-3a[/math]
এখানে [math]a=4[/math] হলে [math]4^{3}-3\cdot4=64-12=52[/math].

Explanation:
সমীকরণটিকে কিউব করলে পাওয়া যায় [math](x+\frac{1}{x})^{3}=x^{3}+\frac{1}{x^{3}}+3(x+\frac{1}{x})[/math]. তাই [math]x^{3}+\frac{1}{x^{3}}=(x+\frac{1}{x})^{3}-3(x+\frac{1}{x})[/math]. দেওয়া মান [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math] বসালে ফলাফল হবে [math]64-12=52[/math]।

Question #524 (ID: 644522)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math](2x^{2}-3)[/math] এর ঘন নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math]8x^{6}-36x^{4}+54x^{2}-27[/math]
খ. [math]8x^{6}+36x^{4}+54x^{2}+27[/math]
গ. [math]8x^{6}-12x^{4}+18x^{2}-27[/math]
ঘ. [math]8x^{6}-48x^{4}+72x^{2}-27[/math]


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](2x^{2}-3)^{3}=(2x^{2})^{3}+3(2x^{2})^{2}(-3)+3(2x^{2})(-3)^{2}+(-3)^{3}[/math]
[math]=8x^{6}+3\cdot4x^{4}\cdot(-3)+3\cdot2x^{2}\cdot9-27[/math]
[math]=8x^{6}-36x^{4}+54x^{2}-27[/math]

Explanation:
বিনোমিয়াল সূত্র ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে: [math](a+b)^{3}=a^{3}+3a^{2}b+3ab^{2}+b^{3}[/math]. এখানে [math]a=2x^{2},\; b=-3[/math]. প্রতিটি পদে a এবং b বসিয়ে গণনা করলে ফল পাওয়া যায়: [math]8x^{6}-36x^{4}+54x^{2}-27[/math]। তাই সঠিক উত্তর ক।

Question #525 (ID: 644520)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^{3}-27[/math] এর উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কোনটি?

Options:
ক. [math](x+3)\left(x^{2}-3 x+9\right)[/math]
খ. [math](x-3)\left(x^{2}+3 x+9\right)[/math]
গ. [math](x-3)\left(x^{2}-3 x+9\right)[/math]
ঘ. [math](x+3)\left(x^{2}+3 x+9\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
সাধারণ সূত্র হল [math]a^{3}-b^{3}=(a-b)\left(a^{2}+a b+b^{2}\right)[/math]. এখানে [math]a=x,\; b=3[/math] নেওলে 
[math]x^{3}-27=(x-3)\left(x^{2}+3x+9\right)[/math].

Explanation:
ঊপরের সূত্র ব্যবহার করলে কেন্দ্রীয় দ্বিমিকে চিহ্নটি ধনাত্মক হয় কারণ সূত্রে মধ্যবর্তী অংশে [math]+ab[/math] থাকে। যাচাই করতে প্রসারণ করলে 
[math](x-3)(x^{2}+3x+9)=x^{3}+3x^{2}+9x-3x^{2}-9x-27=x^{3}-27[/math], যা মূল বহুলকের সমান। তাই সঠিক উত্তর হবে [math](x-3)(x^{2}+3x+9)[/math]।

Question #526 (ID: 644521)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নটির উত্তর দাও :
[math]a+\frac{1}{a}=5[/math] হলে-
[math]a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. 110
খ. 100
গ. 125
ঘ. 115


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math](a+\frac{1}{a})^{3}=a^{3}+3a^{2}\cdot\frac{1}{a}+3a\cdot\frac{1}{a^{2}}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}=a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}+3\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math]
[math]\Rightarrow a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}=(a+\frac{1}{a})^{3}-3\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)=(5)^{3}-3\times5=125-15=110[/math]

Explanation:
কিংবা সরলভাবে বলা যায়, [math]a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}[/math] নির্ণয়ের জন্য আমরা [math](a+\frac{1}{a})^{3}[/math] বিস্তৃত করে ওই পরিচিতি ব্যবহার করেছি: [math](x+y)^{3}=x^{3}+y^{3}+3xy(x+y)[/math] যেখানে এখানে [math]x=a[/math], [math]y=\frac{1}{a}[/math] এবং [math]xy=1[/math]। তাই ফলাফল হচ্ছে [math]110[/math]।
